- Added the permissioned `stage_agent_browser_action_payload` Agent tool for writing validated Browser payload packets to the clipboard.
- Registered the staging tool as a default Agent tool and advertised it through both plugin catalogs beside the read-only composer.

NOTES:
- Staging requires explicit tool authorization and only writes the validated `zed.web_preview.agent_browser_executor_payload.v1` packet to the clipboard; WebPreview import, permission unlock, preflight, focus gates, QA, and receipt logging remain separate requirements.

[2026-05-16] - Agent Browser Payload Composer Tool

ADDED:
- Added the read-only `compose_agent_browser_action_payload` Agent tool for creating validated WebPreview Browser payload packets.
- The tool supports click, type_text, press_key, and scroll payloads with bounded validation for text length, clear-existing support, key allowlists, click counts, mouse buttons, modifiers, and scroll deltas.
- Registered the payload composer as a default Agent tool and advertised it through both the Agent plugin catalog and WebPreview Browser plugin handoff catalog.

NOTES:
- The composer only returns JSON payload packets and handoff instructions; it does not dispatch browser input, import clipboard data, bypass WebPreview permissions, or control external Chrome.

[2026-05-16] - Agent Browser Payload Contract Discovery

ADDED:
- Added Browser plugin action payload contract metadata to both WebPreview handoff catalog and the `list_agent_plugins` tool.
- The contract now exposes the payload bridge schema, executor payload schema, clipboard import action, type/key examples, and safety rules for Agent Browser payload generation.

NOTES:
- This is a discovery-only slice; it does not dispatch browser input or change WebPreview/editor focus routing.

[2026-05-16] - Web Preview Agent Payload Bridge

ADDED:
- Added WebPreview More menu actions to copy an Agent Browser payload bridge, send it to the Agent Panel, or import a JSON/plain-text action payload from the clipboard.
- Added a schema-versioned payload bridge packet that exposes click/type/key/scroll payload templates, the latest action request summary, permission state, and execution rules.
- Added Browser plugin catalog capabilities for payload bridge generation and explicit clipboard payload import.

CHANGED:
- The native type executor can now consume explicit `payload.text` from an imported Agent Browser payload bridge while still requiring the focused target, keyboard-focus gate, QA checklist, and receipt logging.
- Executor readiness and status snapshots now include the latest payload bridge summary so agents can see whether a type payload is ready.

NOTES:
- The payload bridge is a handoff/import layer only; it does not click, type, scroll, press keys, run page scripts, control external Chrome, or bypass WebPreview focus/permission gates.

[2026-05-16] - Web Preview First Native Type Executor

ADDED:
- Added a Windows WebView2 DevTools Protocol type executor that inserts only explicit payload text into the currently focused page input.
- WebPreview's More menu now includes "Run Native Type Executor" and "Run Native Type Executor to Agent".
- Native type execution requires interactive permission, fresh executor context/audit readiness, fresh type preflight, focused-target validation, the shared keyboard-focus gate, explicit payload text, and the native dispatch QA checklist before dispatch.

CHANGED:
- Browser plugin manifests now advertise `browser.action.type` as available when unlocked with an explicit payload requirement.
- Executor readiness now treats click, type, scroll, key, history, and cache-only reset as wired action families, with `type_text` still payload-gated and focused-target-gated.

NOTES:
- This dispatch slice uses WebView2 DevTools Protocol `Input.insertText`; it does not click or focus the target, synthesize OS keyboard events, run page scripts, control external Chrome, or change editor keyboard routing.

[2026-05-16] - Web Preview First Native Key Executor

CHANGED:
- Browser plugin manifests now advertise `browser.action.key` as available when unlocked instead of only planned.
- Executor readiness and QA handoffs now treat native click, scroll, key, history, and cache-only reset as wired while keeping free-form text dispatch disabled.

NOTES:
- This dispatch slice sends only allowlisted keyDown/keyUp events to the in-app WebPreview through WebView2 DevTools Protocol; it does not type arbitrary text, run page scripts, control external Chrome, or change editor keyboard routing.

[2026-05-14] - Icon SVG Rendering And Remote Media Fetch

ADDED:
- `crates/icon_picker/src/icon_representative_bodies.tsv` now embeds representative SVG bodies for hardcoded external icon packs so the default All sets grid can warm real previews without opening every source Iconify JSON file.
- `crates/icon_picker` now warms visible external Iconify SVG previews on a background task and caches the generated SVG files before repainting them into the grid.
- `crates/icon_picker` now indexes Iconify aliases in addition to base icons so alternate icon names from each pack appear in panel search and selected-pack grids.
- `crates/editor` now resolves Iconify aliases when inserting dragged or selected external icons, so alias entries create real SVG assets instead of empty files.
- `crates/icon_picker` and `crates/editor` now apply Iconify alias hFlip, vFlip, and rotate metadata when generating previews or inserted SVG assets.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now writes the initial shadcn rkyv catalog cache on a background task when the cache is missing, keeping first panel construction responsive.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches live no-key remote media rows from Openverse, Wikimedia Commons, NASA, Library of Congress, and Art Institute of Chicago for the active media query/filter.
- `crates/media_panel` now uses shared Zed HTTP client plumbing plus JSON parsing for direct provider results instead of relying only on static sample rows.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches remote media results per active query and media tab so repeated searches and tab switches can repaint immediately.
- `crates/media_panel` now debounces remote provider searches and guards them by generation, preventing stale or partial keystroke searches from repainting the panel.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now reuses available local shadcn screenshot assets as panel row thumbnails, with a small in-memory lookup cache.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches The Met public-domain image results directly through its no-key collection API.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct NASA video and audio assets by resolving NASA collection manifests into playable media files.
- `crates/media_panel` generated remote-browser pages now search Art Institute and The Met no-key APIs and resolve NASA audio/video manifests to playable files.
- `crates/media_panel` remote media rows now carry optional thumbnail URLs so provider preview images can render in native image, video, and audio rows.
- `crates/media_panel` now runs no-key provider fetches concurrently for first-time remote searches while keeping provider-specific error reporting.
- `crates/media_panel` now overlays compact Zed-themed video/audio badges on remote provider thumbnails so playable media does not read as a plain image row.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct Internet Archive image, video, and audio rows by combining no-key advanced search with item metadata/download URLs.
- `crates/media_panel` now caps each remote provider fetch at four seconds so one slow public API cannot block the whole remote media result batch.
- `crates/media_panel` now fetches direct Cleveland Museum of Art CC0 image rows through the no-key open access API.

CHANGED:
- `crates/icon_picker` now caps the in-memory external SVG preview cache to the 4096 most recent icon entries while continuing to rely on the on-disk SVG cache for durable preview reuse.
- `crates/icon_picker` now caps warmed external-icon preview batch signatures to the 128 most recent batches, preventing long icon browsing sessions from accumulating stale warm-signature state.
- `crates/media_panel` now caps cached remote media result sets to the 24 most recent query/filter signatures and pre-sizes the cache containers.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches up to 640 remote provider assets per query while keeping the native panel's visible row cap at 320, giving broader provider coverage without increasing the rendered row window.
- `crates/media_panel` now reuses the active remote-results buffer on cache hits and preallocates remote provider, dedupe, and error buffers for remote media fetches.
- `crates/icon_picker` now keeps selected-pack icon loads scoped to `external_icons_by_pack` instead of extending, sorting, and deduping the broad all-icons list on each individual pack open.
- `crates/icon_picker` now preallocates full external Iconify catalog vectors, pack maps, representative rows, per-pack rows, and SVG body maps from known pack sizes, reducing allocator churn during broad icon search and preview generation.
- `crates/icon_picker`, `crates/font_panel`, `crates/media_panel`, and `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now preallocate bounded visible result buffers before collecting search/filter rows, reducing small allocation churn while typing or switching tabs.
- `crates/icon_picker` now caches built-in Zed icon search text so typed searches do not rebuild `DraggedIconAsset` labels for every Zed icon on each repaint.
- `crates/font_panel` now checks cached lowercase font search text in place instead of cloning the cached `SharedString` for every typed-search font match.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now checks cached catalog search text in place instead of cloning the cached `SharedString` for every typed-search row match.
- `crates/icon_picker` now filters cached or already-warming visible external icons before cloning them for preview warm queues.
- `crates/font_panel` now caches lowercase font search text and only builds visible `FontEntry` rows after a font matches a typed query.
- `crates/media_panel` now matches remote media query terms directly against asset fields instead of formatting and lowercasing a combined searchable string for every remote row.
- `crates/icon_picker` now batches external preview-cache checks with one preview-cache borrow and skips icons that are already warming before queuing another SVG preview batch.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now consumes per-render cached thumbnail URLs when building visible rows, avoiding another thumbnail URL clone per row.
- `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now snapshots visible shadcn preview-image cache hits once per render and passes them into row rendering instead of locking the global thumbnail cache for every visible row.
- `crates/icon_picker` now skips render-path preview-file checks for external icons that are already queued for background SVG preview warming.
- `crates/icon_picker` now limits the empty All Sets representative icon collection to the visible result window instead of extending the full external representative catalog and truncating it afterward.
- `crates/icon_picker`, `crates/font_panel`, `crates/media_panel`, and `crates/shadcn_ui_panel` now consume the already-filtered visible row vectors when rendering tiles/rows instead of cloning each visible item again.
- `crates/media_panel` now computes media-kind counts once per render and shares them with the tab strip and status label, avoiding repeated local/static/remote asset scans.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches local media-kind counts when the media index loads and reuses them for empty-search local totals.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches static direct remote media-kind counts once instead of scanning static remote rows on every render.
- `crates/media_panel` now caches live remote media-kind counts when provider results load or are reused from the remote cache.
- `crates/media_panel` now matches remote media rows by reference and clones only rows that are actually shown.
- `crates/media_panel` now skips remote media search-string construction when the query is empty, reducing idle render work while browsing live provider rows.
- `crates/media_panel` now skips local media search matching when the query is empty, reducing idle render work while browsing large project media indexes.
- `crates/media_panel` now reads and normalizes the panel search query once per render before remote loading and local/remote matching.
- `crates/media_panel` now passes an empty query slice for empty searches instead of allocating split query terms.
